<Rating>5</Rating><Text>My family has trained at Millennia MMA for the last couple of years. My kids take the kid's classes and the trainers are world class and very patient. We left another Martial Arts studio because the techniques they taught, while pretty, wouldn't work in a real fight. The techniques my kids are taught at Millennia would work in a real fight, if, heaven forbid, they found themselves there.  My kids have been instructed by World Champions, UFC Fighters, and Muay Thai Kickboxers that actually lived and trained in Thailand.
My wife takes the cardio kickboxing classes and Muay Thai kickboxing classes and loves it. I've trained in their Jiu jitsu, grappling, MMA, and kickboxing classes. The instructors we've had have all been great, both technically and personality.
The instructors at Millennia compete and that makes a huge difference. They don't teach theory they teach what works.
The gym is big enough that you always have a great variety of training partners and yet the instructors make it a point to know you by name. We've trained alongside UFC, Bellator, and other professional and amateur fighters in the gym. It's a blast to be able to watch your training partners on TV or at a local show on the weekend.
I have and will continue to recommend Millennia to my closest friends.<//Text>< pictures>

< Text>
I sold my bike here. The sales guy is a charm. The service manager is condescending to say the least. The owner seems like a straight up guy, but in the end he's more interested in saving a hundred bucks than making you as a customer feel good. I feel really bad about selling my bike here and I'll tell you why.

I had to sell my bike due to moving out of state. I was offered a price after inspection and repairs which I felt was fair.

They had the bike for 3 weeks for inspection/repair so they had plenty of time to give me a fair quote.

The day I came with the title they said they don't want my bike anymore. But to be "fair" they gave me a new, way lower offer to "take the bike off my hands, or you can just sell it on your own".

After arguing and bickering for 2 hours they finally "agreed" to buy my bike for a lower offer than my original quote. Being desperate not to have to drag this problem as I was moving a couple days later I agreed.

Now why the bad review, expect the obvious above. The reasoning behind the low ball offer was that they had "missed" that the bike had a bad tires, and other things they "needed" to address before being able to sell it. Having it for 3 weeks to make an offer and they missed it, but the day I was there they managed to find all the problems in no time.

Also selling it via consignment they "could not offer it before I put in the money to address these security risks". So that did not make sense.

In the end what happened? They are selling it for $3500 more (minus repairs, no problem with that), and it still has the original bad tire and the other items that needed to be addressed.

Now you know how that makes me feel? Really bad about selling my bike here. Before this ordeal I always loved coming here for my bike needs as I felt it was a cool place with cool people. But this was not cool.

To GP: happy to have the conversation again if you want to have customer satisfaction.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

EDIT: After GPs response to the review

The bike was there for 3 weeks. The same day I brought it in I gave consent to repair the bike. Your sales man would call me later regarding a offer after they knew what needed to be repaired. As he could not give me an offer on the spot as he did not know what the bike needed. So again, you had plenty of time to inspect it.

The reason it was there for 3 weeks was because it took 2 weeks to get a repair quote and offer for the bike because you said you were short on service people due to COVID.  So it only took me 1 week to actually bring in the title after receiving the offer.

Clearly you guys are full of excuses instead of reason, which is why you get the bad review.

And I did like the owner and the sales guy. If I would base my review on that, you would get 5 stars. But you get a bad review because you did not keep your word and dragged it out so I lost money.

It was the service department that took 2 weeks and 2 phone calls to give me a quote for a repair. So if he's mad at me for that, well again then you see what a great attitude you show customers. So again, excuses.

And lastly, the reason I wrote a review in the first place is not all of this. It is because you told me I had to replace the front tire and that is why you low balled my bike. That it was a "safety hazard". Here I go and inspect my bike I sold to you and guess what? The tire is still there. So either you lied or you only care about these "safety hazards" when you can drag the price down. You are untrustworthy.<//Text>

< review>
I bought a new Moto Guzzi California Touring from Paul at GP on June 6, 2020. I think Paul is the owner and while his staff were not always very responsive, he himself was a pleasure to deal with. Overall, I had a good purchase experience. However, 3 weeks later, on June 27, 2020, I discovered that one of the eagle wings on the tank was missing a tab that would ensure it was tightly adhered to the tank. See picture below. I reached out to Paul on the same day via email and asked for his help in getting this defect repaired. I did NOT hear back from Paul and on July 1, 2020, called him. On the tel, he promised me that he would look into a replacement part even though I had not noticed the defect when I took possession of the bike on June 3, 2020. As a follow-up, I sent him the attached picture via email. Between Jul 1, 2020 and July 10, 2020, I did not hear back from Paul so on July 10, 2020, I sent Paul another follow-up email. Today is Aug 4, 2020 and I have still not heard back from him.  After my initial dealings with Paul, I had hoped to have found a dealer that I could refer friends to and also return to myself for future motorcycle purchases. For me, it's valuable to feel that I could build a long-term relationship with a business. But now, in light of my less than satisfying experiences with Paul post-sale, I don't think GP moto is the place for me.<//review>

<Text>GP Motorcycles is simply awesome. I've been riding for 34 years, and bought and sold more motorcycles than I can remember. Dealership experiences are something I've learned to DREAD, nay, HATE. They all seem to have the same high pressure jerks working the sales floor and the same "I don't give a rats ass" finance guys who try to get you to buy a warranty for your insurance for your warranty for your valve stem caps for the low low price of $1,000 per day.

GP Motorcycles is NOT that way and NOT that kind of dealership. The MICHAEL LYNCH was friendly and personable. Once I told him what bike I was interested in, he wanted to know more about me, and why I wanted THAT particular bike. He wanted to make sure I was making a good decision. A quick test ride, a wee' bit of haggling over the price and a deal is struck. While we're waiting for paperwork, insurance documentation and all that, my GF offers to show their salespeople some Microsoft Excel tricks/tips, and the let her. They also keep her engaged in conversation while Michael and I are doing paperwork and such.

In the end, not only did I get a good deal on the Motorcycle I wanted, they included a deal on an unlimited mileage multi-year extended warranty for LESS than half of what other dealers have tried to charge for 1 year/12,000 mile warranties. They included free t-shirts for me and my GF and a KTM Coffee Cup. ON top of all that Michael dug around in the back room and found a GARMIN GPS that fit the mount on that motorcycle as a huge bonus.

ON TOP of all that, they gave the motorcycle a once-over since I was going to be riding it from San Diego to LA.

While waiting for the once-over service, they recommended we go up the street to a GREAT restaurant (and it was an awesome recommendation). Before we even finished lunch, they had the bike done.

Upon returning to the dealership, they greeted us by name and made sure we were both happy before letting us go.

I've honestly never dealt with a dealership this personably, and customer focused. They earned my repeat business and my only EVER 5 star recommendation for a Motorcycle dealership.< /Text></record></dataset><record>

I usually get an outstanding haircut here. This time I went very early and I was the second customer of the day and no one was behind me.

Needless to say my hair wouldn't lay down correctly because it was still dirty and with the conditioner that made it sticky.

When she took me back to her station she tried to break speed records cutting my hair.  I have weird hair, I need the top of my head to be shorter than the sides so that it will stand up and hide how thin my hair is.  The sides by my ears need to be super short.  I hate to have to tuck my hair behind my ears.

Long story short, my hair was not even, especially around my ears.  I ended up telling her that it was ok just so that I could escape. I hope that she gets the idea, not that I am just cheap.
Next time I will wait for the manager.</Review>

<Review>The feeling is at about 3.5 stars!

We came as they were closing lunch time (3pm) on Christmas day but they were nice to accommodate us anyways.

Service was super fast and friendly and the place overall is neat. Portions are quite big per person and pricing is good.

Between the four of us we ordered:

- fish 65
- prawn biryani
- egg curry
- non veg thali
- steamed idlis
- mysore masala dosa

I didn't try the fish 65 but the others weren't very pleased with it. Egg curry was good for our vegetarian friend. Non veg thali had everything in it with beautiful flavors and you could distinguish the different flavors from the different meats. Idlis were fluffy and quite soft but the mysore masala dosa was too soggy :( so that was a let down. Prawn biryani was so tasty and flavorful but quite spicy so ask for yogurt and lots of fresh cut limes to put on top to ease the spice levels.

Food is spicy and full on masala so I would skip dinner and stick to lunch so you can digest your food. It is definitely not a place where I see myself coming too often since the food is heavy and too spicy even for Indians themselves ;) bring napkins for tears and running nose :P< /Review><Resp>None</Resp><GmapID>0x808fb587d773b913:0xb22f55fc5bbe60c7<//GmapID><userid>107802058118069961657</userid>< Pics>

< Review>
Very busy Indian place. Here you will get mostly South Indian cuisine, however North Indian and the indo-Chinese foods are also available. The starters I ate were Gobi manchurian and chicken lollipop. Those were absolute yum! In the main course I ordered some spicy chicken ( May be, the pepper chicken chettinad style or similar). This was quite on the spicier side. So if you cannot stand with the hotness, ask them to make it low/ medium spicy. Ordered naan and the appam to pair with the chicken dish. The naan was kinda okay, but the appam was great. One of my friends ate the masala dosha, which I would hardly rate as 3 out of 5!</Review>

</record></dataset><record>
< text>
A great place to have some really awesome chettinad (and surprisingly Indo-Chinese) food in the Bay Area. Although Indian food is great in South Bay, this is one of my favorite spots.

Location and Ambience: The place is located in a shopping complex with other shops and food joints and therefore it has plenty of parking spots. The inside of the restaurant is alright but not great by bay area standards. We got a table near the front which was pretty comfortable. The place isn't too loud.

Wait times: Although I hear wait times are horrible at this spot, I've never had problem getting a spot (even for larger groups), at least during lunch/weekends.

Service: The staff was friendly and very accommodating. 2 members of our group were delayed. Yet they allowed the rest of our group to sit and order. We also needed some time to order since we had a large group, and all the while the staff was completely okay with it. The food arrived pretty quickly, although one dish at a time, which was slightly annoying, but the taste made up for it.

Food: I am leaving 5 stars just for the food. Be warned, chettinad food is supposed to be spicy, so expect that in anything you order. I loved the authenticity of the food, something that a lot of places miss out on. The Indo-Chinese is spot on. I recommend the Vegetable Manchurian (Dry), Chicken Lollypop, Chilly Chicken (Dry), and the Fried rice. And from the chettinad menu, I recommend prawn masala, mutton sukka varuval, kothu parotha (mutton or chicken), fish curry (or mutton curry) with appam, biryani and the non-veg meal. After all of this food, i was ready for a nap. The filter coffee, buttermilk and lime soda were all great companions to the crazy lunch we had.

Overall, I give this place 5 stars, just for the food. If you want to have a great time, you need to ignore everything and just focus on the food here.< /text>

<user_id>102288761280391594138< /user_id><Name>Sashwat Singh< /Name>< time>
1527722016345<//time>
< rate>
4<//rate>
< review>
Unsure why this place only has 3 stars. I guess it's probably due to snobby Californians who refuse to rate a chain more than 3 stars.

Only reason why I docked 1 star from this place is because of 1) slow service/lack of attentiveness and 2) LACK OF CHEESE IN THE CHEESE NAAN!

Every time I come here, I ask for extra cheese in the cheese naan. They happily charge me $1 for extra cheese, but I actually receive extra cheese in it about 30% of the time. Even when I specifically state "please put lots and lots and lots of cheese in the cheese naan", I'll generally get little to no cheese in it. Trust me, when they load it up with cheese, this is an incredible dish. One time they put an adequate amount of cheese in it and the only other time they did after that was when I told them "Last time you charged me for extra cheese and there was basically no cheese in it. Please, please, please make sure you put A LOT of cheese in it".

Now that I'm done with my cheese rant, onto the food. The food is amazing here.

Chicken/Paneer 65: 4.5/5 - not super spicy like most chicken 65, but delicious. More like chicken pakodas with a bit of spice. Paneer 65 is also great. Interested in trying Mushroom 65, but haven't given it a chance yet since it's the same price as Paneer 65... can't justify buying at that pricepoint.

Hot & Sour Soup: 5/5 - extremely spicy and flavorful. I can come here and order only this 1 by 2 and leave completely satisfied.

Cheese Naan: 2/5 when they skimp on the cheese; 5/5 when they load it up.

Chicken Chettinad: 5/5 - Haven't tasted it here because I'm not a huge fan of the dish in general, but my wife loves it. She gets the combo, which comes with a smaller portion of chicken and a side of parotta. This is a great call, because I'm not a fan of chicken chettinad and she doesn't eat much -- perfect portion!

Goat Biryani: 4/5 - Extremely flavorful biryani, but unfortunately the goat pieces are a bit on the chewy side + no marrow bones :(

Black Pepper Chicken Kabab: 2.5/5 -- These are well cooked, but I only recommend them if you're a HUGE fan of black pepper. They use whole peppercorns and, for me, they were a bit overwhelming.

Pro-Tip: Order the Chicken 65 Biryani. It's a good call if you're trying to save some $$ and are craving biryani and chicken 65.

The server we always get is SUPER SUPER polite. Love the guy. Unfortunately, the food comes out at a snails pace... worth the wait though. Main qualm about this place is they need to just get their act together and load up the cheese on that cheese naan!<//review>

< Text>
Delicious Lunch Thalis!!

We were here for lunch and were served one of the delicious south Indian non-veg thalis around bay area.
What we ordered:
Anjappar Popular Non Veg Meal- comes with Chettinad chicken masala, mutton curry, fish curry, three types of vegetables, chapati, rasam, white rice, sweet, yogurt, pickle and pappad. Delicious Chettinad flavours.
Chicken Meal- Comes with Chicken curry and all other veggie items above- Equally spicy and delicious. Can't ask for more.
Meal were enough to fill the craving appetites.

Restaurant is pretty decent in size and the serving was faster in comparison.
Will try other items on the menu soon.</Text>
